<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><strong>World Travel Guides You Can Trust</strong></h1>


<p><em>We are Tim and Michelle, a South-Florida based couple who founded this website to document and share our travel experiences with the world in hopes of helping people make better decisions as they plan and book their travels.  We use first hand experiences to be your world travel guides and help you find the best things to do, eat, and see while traveling the world.</em></p>


<div class="wp-block-columns are-vertically-aligned-top no-bottom is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column is-vertically-aligned-top is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:100%">
<div class="wp-block-group is-content-justification-center is-nowrap is-layout-flex wp-container-core-group-is-layout-94bc23d7 wp-block-group-is-layout-flex"><div class="wp-block-image aligncenter">
<figure class="size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" width="320" height="262" src="https://www.allworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/Tim-Michelle-Travel-Blog.jpeg" alt="All World Travel" class="wp-image-1008010" style="width:539px;height:auto" srcset="https://www.allworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/Tim-Michelle-Travel-Blog.jpeg 320w, https://www.allworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/02/Tim-Michelle-Travel-Blog-300x246.jpeg 300w" sizes="(max-width: 320px) 100vw, 320px" /></figure></div></div>
</div>
</div>


<p></p>


<p>We aim to provide you unbiased travel experiences, trip reports, restaurant and bar reviews, and tips to help you make better decisions when you book trips and excursions.&nbsp; We also have many guest authors helping us create what we hope becomes a top resources for travelers.</p>


<p>Both of us have careers that allow us to work remote, allowing us to make frequent updates to the website documenting and reviewing our experiences in real time!&nbsp;</p>


<p>While we call Fort Lauderdale home, (as you’ll see a lot of our favorites highlighted in our “<a href="https://www.allworld.com/category/best-of-all-world/" data-lasso-id="24050">Best of All World</a>” section which points out restaurants, dive bars, and hotels wherever we roam,) we’re often on the road and this blog helps share those experiences with the masses.</p>


<p>And while you are here, make sure to download our FREE ebook called “<a href="https://www.allworld.com/travel-hacks-tips/" data-lasso-id="24051">All World Travel Hacks</a>.” It’s FULL of actionable moves you can make to get discounted and free travel on airlines, hotels, and more.</p>


<p class="no-bottom">Looking for more exposure for your business? <a href="https://www.allworld.com/work-with-us/" data-lasso-id="20346">Learn more about how you can work with us</a> and grow your business through our global reach.</p>
</div></div>
